function delete_ded1()    
for a=1,65635,1 do
local obj=alife():object(a)
if obj and string.find(obj:name(),"esc_ded_1") then     
alife():release(obj,true)
end
end
end

function bind(obj)
  obj:bind_object(bolt_binder(obj))
end

class "bolt_binder" ( object_binder )

function bolt_binder:__init( obj, ini ) super( obj )
  self.ini         = ini
end

function bolt_binder:update( delta )
  object_binder.update( self, delta )
end

function bolt_binder:net_spawn( data )
  if not object_binder.net_spawn( self, data ) then
    return false
  end
  
  dxii_moe_govno.debug_print("booolt")

  return true
end

function bolt_binder:net_destroy()
  dxii_moe_govno.debug_print("nooo")
  
  object_binder.net_destroy( self )
end
